I've been to another location of theirs that has an excellent reputation. This location in Tracy is no less. We ordered a variety of dishes, chicken, beef, lamb and all were cooked to perfection, the seasoning etc. The  chapli kabob, bolani, mantu, again all done very well. I felt the bolani was one of the best prepared I've had in a while. I would put this restaurant high on my list of restaurants that serve similar dishes. The particular night of our visit, the service was friendly and excellent. Don't hesitate to vist if you are searching for Afghan food.<//Text>

[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMvqxedUZS1D8hKXHSaWkGoCifMbCVJCMYw-Zs=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipPvks2LKG4MkocsNp6iJp3WwnbMO-d4B_QdMKk=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipPKL_KM-sZUWhP3uxHiTpxvvI79RTHno4LwCxA=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMHf9f_Q548PDbctYKEbslSKEGtrHKBbs1F6lw=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipPC2o2PUjA2fb26wHWIxiB2LsxqltfuvCCZjZ8=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]< /Pics>
< Text>
We came on a Thursday night and there were 3 other tables. The food took a while to come out, so just be prepared. We each got a chicken pea and potato appetizer for free, but I didn't eat much because it was super sour.

We got:
*Potato Bolani ($9.99, 3.5 stars) - I've discovered that all Bolani comes with large portions :) however, this was definitely the biggest I've seen (see picture). We've had it for 3 meals already, and there is still 1/3 left. The Bolani is pretty blend, so it's a good food to eat with dips or meat.

*Chaplee combo (4.5 stars) - Chaplee is ground meat (usually beef) formed in thin patties and seasoned with chili flakes and other spices. The version here was delicious because of the crispy browned edges. I would stuff a small piece inside the Bolani and dipped it in yogurt sauce.

*Kabuli pallow (3.5 stars) - This is one of my favorite Afghan dishes, a traditional dish with tender shank of lamb buries under a mountain of seasoned basmati rice with raisins and carrots. This dish lacks some deep flavors, but the lamb shank was very tender, and there was a little bone marrow in the bone. Yum!< /Text>

<response>None</response>< text>
It’s unbelievable place. I’ve been there once but if I could I would go everyday and I’m sure that I will not be tired of universal studio. The best way to save money it’s to buy tickets online, you can save up to 15$ there compare to if you are buying ticket right on entrance. Lines to attractions are big, about 30-40 min wait that’s why it’s better to go early in the morning. It’s will be less people and you will have more time to explore everything. < review>
This is the nearest train station to my house and I am so grateful for it. The North Hollywood station one stop up sees a much higher volume of riders, more questionable activities in the immediate area, and the train often sits idle for several minutes before taking off.

At Universal, I always feel safe because it is well lit, there are often LAPD officers patrolling the area, and a large majority of the traffic is tourists coming to visit Universal Studios. I also am so grateful for the number of ticket machines available. The decor and style of the platform adds a little unique flavor.</review>

I've used this Tesla Supercharger location twice in the past 2 weeks and I've had problems both times. Last week I pulled in and grabbed one of the chargers near the front of the hotel. I plugged in and unplugged in a few times and it would not start charging. Since there were a lot of open spots, I moved my car to another stall and it was able to charge properly.

Today I visited this location again and charged my car near the middle. I've had multiple interruptions where the car would stop charging. I did a combination of waiting to see if it would start back on its own or unplug and plug back in. Overall, it was not as smooth as other charging locations because of this issue.

At this location, you have an option to walk into the hotel to use the bathroom or buy some food. The location is near the freeway exit.<//review>

<Text>Great repair and excellent customer service by Yossi! My 6 year old Zacconi Espresso Baby lever machine purchased from Christopher at Thomas Cara in SF (no more) developed a leak from the group head when the lever was down and could not build pressure.

Reached out to Yossi via email and received an immediate response and coordinated drop off at his Richmond shop.

Quote was for $321 for:

Service Complete tune up: Take machine apart, remove group head
assembly, Remove steam valve, and deep clean. Replace
group head gasket kit + steam valve gaskets and install
everything back and test for leaks.

Parts
New OEM group gasket kit

Parts
New OEM steam valve gasket kit

Approved and turn around time for repair was ~2 weeks. Got lucky since he had had another Zacconi in and had ordered multiple parts so didn't have to wait the ~6 weeks for parts from Italy.

Communication throughout the whole repair was excellent and Yossi was flexible on pickup accommodating a weekend pick-up.

My "Baby" is restored to its amazing self.

Yossi includes photos and video of the process which is helpful.

100% recommend!!!<//Text><pics>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMZumrf8mqi62R3rsWX0BgylbTuWREyfzH_tmpA=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipOeY5r5jP1qwT8Oy6GzKtMSr_KppHqssH-lg3zA=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipP2JI6STfh_Ag2jhvf4ICFoNStSoeD9TBvCiG0P=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipPjnTyDecX_ZEJWIomtrnmb8soBBEFnIQF-cG6Z=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipO402KETTC6L-APCbtW5HW2PXcDW5PVU56dT165=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipOrblEkArAmSq6Hn7uX3mnIxg5zoJAXDMU3ESep=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]</pics>< Response>

It worked well, but had a slightly bent steam wand, some rust inside the base, and a pressure release valve that didn't budge. I had some work done on it a couple of years ago to replace the base and deal to deal with a leak that popped up. It was working well until a few weeks ago when another leak popped up. I decided to bring it in to OZ Espresso.

<review>I've been to a lot of places that serve either Tex Mex or "Authentic" Mexican food as I have family in the easy bay, live in the north bay and work in SF.

Most places rely too much on having the best sauce or whatever their particular spin is but this place gets the whole burrito right. <Text>This is a single star of bitterness.

I used to eat at the Green Chile in the city when it started because it was a block from my friend's apartment, and became our hung over breakfast burrito spot. Over the years I have watched it become more and more popular, but also more and more expensive. The food is good, and the ingredients are high quality, but if you are looking for a good burrito, there are other places in Marin.

Unfortunately, as of today I will officially never eat here again. I went to the San Rafael location for a burrito (steak, sour cream, guac) after a long Green Chile hiatus, and they charged me a shocking $20+, with no drink. The Bay is expensive, but that is just a Marin gringo rip off. This food, though it is tasty, is simply not worth the price tag. Some restaurants open in Marin just thinking that because people in the area might have money, they can charge whatever they want. This is how a lot of places go out of business around here, because in reality people are tight with their money, and if the value isn't there, they go elsewhere... I've seen it a lot growing up. Anyway, boo hoo, but I would suggest Picante in the Canal, or Mi Pueblo in San Anselmo.< /Text><response>None</response><rate>1</rate><name>Jon Price</name>< date>
1484009911065</date>
